+/*
+ * This test replicates the exact scenario described in the PR:
+ * 
+ * 1. First call coro_rpc_client::connect() to address A.
+ * 2. Then the server that listens to A crashes.
+ * 3. Call coro_rpc_client::connect() to address B.
+ * 
+ * Before the fix: The client would try to reconnect to A even though B was provided.
+ * After the fix: The client correctly connects to B.
+ */
+
+#include <ylt/coro_rpc/coro_rpc_client.hpp>
+#include <ylt/coro_rpc/coro_rpc_server.hpp>
+#include <async_simple/coro/SyncAwait.h>
+#include <iostream>
+#include <thread>
+#include <chrono>
+
+using namespace coro_rpc;
+using namespace async_simple::coro;
+using namespace std::chrono_literals;
+
+std::string identify_server(std::string server_name) {
+    return "I am " + server_name;
+}
+
+int main() {
+    std::cout << "=== Replicating PR scenario ===" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << std::endl;
+    
+    // Step 1: Setup servers
+    unsigned short port_A = 19901;
+    unsigned short port_B = 19902;
+    
+    std::cout << "Setting up server A on port " << port_A << std::endl;
+    coro_rpc_server server_A(1, port_A);
+    server_A.register_handler<identify_server>();
+    auto res_A = server_A.async_start();
+    if (res_A.hasResult()) {
+        std::cerr << "FAILED: Server A couldn't start" << std::endl;
+        return 1;
+    }
+    
+    std::cout << "Setting up server B on port " << port_B << std::endl;
+    coro_rpc_server server_B(1, port_B);
+    server_B.register_handler<identify_server>();
+    auto res_B = server_B.async_start();
+    if (res_B.hasResult()) {
+        std::cerr << "FAILED: Server B couldn't start" << std::endl;
+        server_A.stop();
+        return 1;
+    }
+    
+    std::this_thread::sleep_for(100ms);
+    
+    // Step 2: Create client and connect to address A
+    coro_rpc_client client;
+    std::string address_A = "127.0.0.1:" + std::to_string(port_A);
+    
+    std::cout << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "Step 1: First call coro_rpc_client::connect() to address A (" << address_A << ")" << std::endl;
+    auto ec1 = syncAwait(client.connect(address_A));
+    if (ec1) {
+        std::cerr << "FAILED: Couldn't connect to server A: " << ec1.message() << std::endl;
+        server_A.stop();
+        server_B.stop();
+        return 1;
+    }
+    std::cout << "  ✓ Successfully connected to address A" << std::endl;
+    
+    // Verify we're connected to server A
+    auto result_A = syncAwait(client.call<identify_server>("Server_A"));
+    if (!result_A) {
+        std::cerr << "FAILED: Couldn't call RPC on server A: " << result_A.error().msg << std::endl;
+        server_A.stop();
+        server_B.stop();
+        return 1;
+    }
+    std::cout << "  ✓ RPC response from server: " << result_A.value() << std::endl;
+    
+    // Step 3: The server that listens to A crashes
+    std::cout << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "Step 2: Then the server that listens to A crashes" << std::endl;
+    client.close();
+    server_A.stop();
+    std::cout << "  ✓ Server A crashed (stopped)" << std::endl;
+    std::this_thread::sleep_for(100ms);
+    
+    // Step 4: Call coro_rpc_client::connect() to address B
+    std::string address_B = "127.0.0.1:" + std::to_string(port_B);
+    
+    std::cout << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "Step 3: Call coro_rpc_client::connect() to address B (" << address_B << ")" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  Note: B is different from A (port " << port_B << " != port " << port_A << ")" << std::endl;
+    
+    auto ec2 = syncAwait(client.connect(address_B));
+    if (ec2) {
+        std::cerr << std::endl;
+        std::cerr << "FAILED: Couldn't connect to server B: " << ec2.message() << std::endl;
+        std::cerr << "Current client config: " << client.get_host() << ":" << client.get_port() << std::endl;
+        std::cerr << std::endl;
+        std::cerr << "This would indicate the BUG is present:" << std::endl;
+        std::cerr << "  The client tried to connect to A (port " << port_A << ") instead of B (port " << port_B << ")" << std::endl;
+        std::cerr << "  even though the input address was B!" << std::endl;
+        server_B.stop();
+        return 1;
+    }
+    std::cout << "  ✓ Successfully connected to address B" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  ✓ Client config correctly shows: " << client.get_host() << ":" << client.get_port() << std::endl;
+    
+    // Verify we're actually connected to server B (not A)
+    auto result_B = syncAwait(client.call<identify_server>("Server_B"));
+    if (!result_B) {
+        std::cerr << "FAILED: Couldn't call RPC on server B: " << result_B.error().msg << std::endl;
+        server_B.stop();
+        return 1;
+    }
+    std::cout << "  ✓ RPC response from server: " << result_B.value() << std::endl;
+    
+    if (result_B.value() == "I am Server_B") {
+        std::cout << "  ✓ Confirmed: We are connected to server B, not server A!" << std::endl;
+    }
+    
+    client.close();
+    server_B.stop();
+    
+    std::cout << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "=== SUCCESS: The fix works correctly! ===" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "The client successfully:" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  1. Connected to address A" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  2. Handled server A crash" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  3. Connected to address B (different from A)" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  4. Communicated with server B" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "The bug described in the PR has been fixed!" << std::endl;
+    
+    return 0;
+}

+/*
+ * Simple logic test to verify the fix allows reconnecting to different addresses
+ * This tests the core logic without needing to compile and run the full test suite
+ */
+
+#include <iostream>
+#include <string>
+
+// Simulating the old behavior
+void test_old_behavior() {
+    std::string config_host;
+    std::string config_port;
+    
+    // First connection to address A (127.0.0.1:8801)
+    std::string host1 = "127.0.0.1";
+    std::string port1 = "8801";
+    
+    if (config_host.empty()) {
+        config_host = host1;
+    }
+    if (config_port.empty()) {
+        config_port = port1;
+    }
+    
+    std::cout << "Old behavior - First connect:" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  Requested: " << host1 << ":" << port1 << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  Config: " << config_host << ":" << config_port << std::endl;
+    
+    // Second connection to address B (127.0.0.1:8802)
+    std::string host2 = "127.0.0.1";
+    std::string port2 = "8802";
+    
+    if (config_host.empty()) {
+        config_host = host2;
+    }
+    if (config_port.empty()) {
+        config_port = port2;
+    }
+    
+    std::cout << "Old behavior - Second connect (different address):" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  Requested: " << host2 << ":" << port2 << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  Config: " << config_host << ":" << config_port << std::endl;
+    
+    if (config_host != host2 || config_port != port2) {
+        std::cout << "  BUG: Config still points to old address!" << std::endl;
+    }
+    std::cout << std::endl;
+}
+
+// Simulating the new behavior
+void test_new_behavior() {
+    std::string config_host;
+    std::string config_port;
+    
+    // First connection to address A (127.0.0.1:8801)
+    std::string host1 = "127.0.0.1";
+    std::string port1 = "8801";
+    
+    config_host = host1;
+    config_port = port1;
+    
+    std::cout << "New behavior - First connect:" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  Requested: " << host1 << ":" << port1 << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  Config: " << config_host << ":" << config_port << std::endl;
+    
+    // Second connection to address B (127.0.0.1:8802)
+    std::string host2 = "127.0.0.1";
+    std::string port2 = "8802";
+    
+    config_host = host2;
+    config_port = port2;
+    
+    std::cout << "New behavior - Second connect (different address):" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  Requested: " << host2 << ":" << port2 << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "  Config: " << config_host << ":" << config_port << std::endl;
+    
+    if (config_host == host2 && config_port == port2) {
+        std::cout << "  FIXED: Config correctly updated to new address!" << std::endl;
+    }
+    std::cout << std::endl;
+}

+    std::cout << "=== Testing reconnect to different address logic ===" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << std::endl;
+    
+    test_old_behavior();
+    test_new_behavior();
+    
+    std::cout << "=== Test complete ===" << std::endl;
+    return 0;
+}

+/*
+ * Test case to reproduce the issue where coro_rpc_client cannot
+ * reconnect to a different address
+ */
+
+#include <async_simple/coro/Lazy.h>
+#include <async_simple/coro/SyncAwait.h>
+#include <iostream>
+#include <ylt/coro_rpc/coro_rpc_client.hpp>
+#include <ylt/coro_rpc/coro_rpc_server.hpp>
+#include <thread>
+#include <chrono>
+
+using namespace coro_rpc;
+using namespace async_simple::coro;
+using namespace std::chrono_literals;
+
+// Simple RPC function for testing
+std::string echo(std::string msg) {
+    return msg;
+}
+
+int main() {
+    std::cout << "Starting test for reconnecting to different address..." << std::endl;
+    
+    // Create two servers on different ports
+    unsigned short port1 = 9801;
+    unsigned short port2 = 9802;
+    
+    coro_rpc_server server1(1, port1);
+    server1.register_handler<echo>();
+    auto res1 = server1.async_start();
+    if (res1.hasResult()) {
+        std::cerr << "Server 1 failed to start on port " << port1 << std::endl;
+        return 1;
+    }
+    
+    coro_rpc_server server2(1, port2);
+    server2.register_handler<echo>();
+    auto res2 = server2.async_start();
+    if (res2.hasResult()) {
+        std::cerr << "Server 2 failed to start on port " << port2 << std::endl;
+        return 1;
+    }
+    
+    std::this_thread::sleep_for(100ms);  // Give servers time to start
+    
+    // Create a client and connect to server1
+    coro_rpc_client client;
+    
+    std::cout << "Test 1: Connecting to server1 (127.0.0.1:" << port1 << ")..." << std::endl;
+    auto ec1 = syncAwait(client.connect("127.0.0.1", std::to_string(port1)));
+    if (ec1) {
+        std::cerr << "Failed to connect to server1: " << ec1.message() << std::endl;
+        return 1;
+    }
+    std::cout << "Connected to server1 successfully" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "Current host: " << client.get_host() << ", port: " << client.get_port() << std::endl;
+    
+    // Test RPC call on server1
+    auto result1 = syncAwait(client.call<echo>("Hello Server1"));
+    if (!result1) {
+        std::cerr << "RPC call to server1 failed: " << result1.error().msg << std::endl;
+        return 1;
+    }
+    std::cout << "RPC call to server1 result: " << result1.value() << std::endl;
+    
+    // Close connection to server1
+    client.close();
+    std::cout << "Closed connection to server1" << std::endl;
+    
+    // Stop server1 to simulate a server crash
+    server1.stop();
+    std::cout << "Stopped server1 to simulate crash" << std::endl;
+    std::this_thread::sleep_for(100ms);
+    
+    // Try to connect to server2 (a different address)
+    std::cout << "\nTest 2: Attempting to connect to server2 (127.0.0.1:" << port2 << ")..." << std::endl;
+    auto ec2 = syncAwait(client.connect("127.0.0.1", std::to_string(port2)));
+    if (ec2) {
+        std::cerr << "Failed to connect to server2: " << ec2.message() << std::endl;
+        std::cout << "Current host: " << client.get_host() << ", port: " << client.get_port() << std::endl;
+        std::cerr << "BUG REPRODUCED: Client tried to connect to old address instead of new one!" << std::endl;
+        return 1;
+    }
+    std::cout << "Connected to server2 successfully" << std::endl;
+    std::cout << "Current host: " << client.get_host() << ", port: " << client.get_port() << std::endl;
+    
+    // Test RPC call on server2
+    auto result2 = syncAwait(client.call<echo>("Hello Server2"));
+    if (!result2) {
+        std::cerr << "RPC call to server2 failed: " << result2.error().msg << std::endl;
+        return 1;
+    }
+    std::cout << "RPC call to server2 result: " << result2.value() << std::endl;
+    
+    // Test reconnecting to the same address again
+    client.close();
+    std::cout << "\nTest 3: Reconnecting to server2 (same address)..." << std::endl;
+    auto ec3 = syncAwait(client.connect("127.0.0.1", std::to_string(port2)));
+    if (ec3) {
+        std::cerr << "Failed to reconnect to server2: " << ec3.message() << std::endl;
+        return 1;
+    }
+    std::cout << "Reconnected to server2 successfully" << std::endl;
+    
+    client.close();
+    server2.stop();
+    
+    std::cout << "\n=== All tests passed! ===" << std::endl;
+    return 0;
+}
